<p><b>Kyobashi Station</b> <span style="font-weight: normal">(<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja" xml:lang="ja">京橋駅</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i>Kyōbashi-eki</i><sup class="t_nihongo_help noprint"><a href="/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" title="Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color: #00e; font: bold 80% sans-serif; text-decoration: none; padding: 0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup>)</span> is a railway station in the <a href="/wiki/Ky%C5%8Dbashi#Osaka" title="Kyōbashi">Kyōbashi</a> district of <a href="/wiki/J%C5%8Dt%C5%8D-ku,_Osaka" title="Jōtō-ku, Osaka">Jōtō-ku</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miyakojima-ku,_Osaka" title="Miyakojima-ku, Osaka">Miyakojima-ku</a> <a href="/wiki/Osaka" title="Osaka">Osaka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lines">Lines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ky%C5%8Dbashi_Station_(Osaka)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Lines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li>JR West
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Osaka_Loop_Line" title="Osaka Loop Line">Osaka Loop Line</a></li>

</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Tōzai and Gakkentoshi Lines form a combined service line in practice.</p>

<li>Keihan Railway (KH04)

</ul>

<p>As of 2010, Kyobashi was the fourth busiest station in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JR_West" title="JR West">JR West</a> network after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Osaka_Station" title="Osaka Station">Osaka Station</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kyoto_Station" title="Kyoto Station">Kyoto Station</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tennoji_Station" title="Tennoji Station">Tennoji Station</a>.</p>
<p>The station was built in 1895 as part of the Osaka Railway (now Osaka Loop Line) extension from Tennoji to Umeda (now Osaka Station). The Katamachi Line station was opened in 1912.</p>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Bombing_of_Osaka" title="Bombing of Osaka">bombing of Osaka</a> on August 14, 1945, a one-ton bomb directly struck the Katamachi Line platform and killed 700 to 800 evacuees. Kyobashi was one of the last sites to be bombed in Japan during World War II, followed only by the bombing of Akita, later the same day. A memorial was erected on the site in 1947, and anniversary services have been held at the station every year since 1955.</p>
<p>The JR Tozai Line opened in 1997, at which point Kyobashi became a terminal for both the Tozai Line and Katamachi Line.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Layout">Layout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ky%C5%8Dbashi_Station_(Osaka)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Layout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p>Kyobashi is the busiest station in the Keihan network. The Keihan terminal was originally built in 1910 and relocated twice in 1932 and 1969.</p>
<p>This station is the transfer station between the Keihan Line and the Nakanoshima Line. The connections are follows:</p>
<dl>
<dd>eastbound: trains from Nakanoshima ←→ trains from Yodoyabashi</dd>
<dd>westbound: trains for Nakanoshima ←→ trains for Yodoyabashi</dd>
</dl>

<tr>
<th style="padding:5px; text-align:center; vertical-align:center; color:white; background-color:#5ba094"><span style="font-size:110%; padding:0 5px;">Station layout<br/>
(Keihan)</span></th>
</tr>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Layout_2">Layout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ky%C5%8Dbashi_Station_(Osaka)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Layout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>2 island platforms on the 4th level serve 4 tracks.</p>
<table border="0" cellpadding="3|-" cellspacing="0">
<tr>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="30"><b>1, 2</b></td>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="145"><span style="color: #6c3">■</span> Keihan Line</td>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="430">for <a href="/wiki/Hirakatashi_Station" title="Hirakatashi Station">Hirakatashi</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chushojima_Station" title="Chushojima Station">Chushojima</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sanjo_Station_(Kyoto)" title="Sanjo Station (Kyoto)">Sanjo</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Demachiyanagi_Station" title="Demachiyanagi Station">Demachiyanagi</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="30"><b>3, 4</b></td>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="145"><span style="color: #6c3">■</span> Keihan Line</td>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="430">for <a href="/wiki/Yodoyabashi_Station" title="Yodoyabashi Station">Yodoyabashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nakanoshima_Station_(Osaka)" title="Nakanoshima Station (Osaka)">Nakanoshima</a></td>

<p>The Osaka Municipal Subway network was extended to Kyobashi in 1990 when the Tsurumi-Ryokuchi Line opened between Kyobashi and <a href="/wiki/Tsurumi-ryokuchi_Station" title="Tsurumi-ryokuchi Station">Tsurumi-ryokuchi Station</a> to serve <a href="/wiki/Expo_%2790" title="Expo '90">Expo '90</a> visitors.</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Layout_3">Layout</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ky%C5%8Dbashi_Station_(Osaka)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Layout">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>An island platform on the 3rd basement fenced with <a href="/wiki/Platform_screen_doors" title="Platform screen doors">platform gates</a> serves 2 tracks.</p>
<table border="0" cellpadding="3|-" cellspacing="0">
<tr>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="30"><b>1</b></td>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="145"><span style="color: #a9cc51">■</span> Nagahori Tsurumi-ryokuchi Line</td>
<td style="border-top:solid 1px gray;border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="430">eastbound for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kadomaminami_Station" title="Kadomaminami Station">Kadomaminami</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="30"><b>2</b></td>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="145"><span style="color: #a9cc51">■</span> Nagahori Tsurumi-ryokuchi Line</td>
<td style="border-bottom:solid 1px gray;" width="430">westbound for <a href="/wiki/Morinomiya_Station" title="Morinomiya Station">Morinomiya</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shinsaibashi_Station" title="Shinsaibashi Station">Shinsaibashi</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taisho_Station_(Osaka)" title="Taisho Station (Osaka)">Taisho</a></td>
</tr>
</table>
